And make an incision between the privy and the vulva not in the middle but to the side of the left haunch and let the incision be on the same stone and your finger in the privy and you press it outwards tautly so that the incision is wide outside and narrow inside as much as possible for the stone to come out from it.
No bigger lest perhaps you press the finger which is in the privy the stone at the incision so that it comes out without difficulty, and know that there may be from the stone what has angles and letters making its exit difficult therefore.
And from it smooth like the plum and rolled easily it is easy to exit, so what was from it that has angles and letters increase in the incision a little if it does not come out this way then it is necessary to contrive upon it either by grasping it with a pair of pliers which are firm and its end is like a knife.
To hold onto the stone so that it does not slip from it or perhaps you introduce under it a fine tool with a bent end, if you were unable to do this on it then widen the incision a little if something of blood overcomes you cut it off with the saffron.
If there are more than one, first push the larger one into the mouth of the bladder then make a cut on it and then push the smaller one after that. And you should do likewise if there are more than two. If it is very large, he does not know how to make a large cut on it because he exposes the patient to one of two things.
Either he will die or there will always be a dribbling of urine because the place will not heal together at all. But try to push it until it comes out or manage to break it with instruments until you get it out completely.
And if you have finished your work, wash the wound with vinegar and patience and honey and tighten it and put over it a bandage wet with oil and syrup or rose ointment and cold water to calm the hot swelling then the patient lies on his back and do not loosen the bandage until the third day.
And if it loosens, the wound drains with water and oil then treat it with palm ointment and balsam ointment until it heals. If a hot swelling appears in the wound, along with pain and such like, for example, if blood clots in the bladder and urine retention occurs, which is known by the blood coming out with the urine.
Then insert your finger into the wound and remove that blood because if it remains, it calls for the bladder to become corrupt and infected. Then wash the wound with vinegar, water, and salt and treat each type according to its kind until it heals.
It is necessary during all times of treatment that the thighs be bound and brought together to secure the medicines placed on the area. If the stone is small and got stuck in the urethra and urine retention occurred, treat it with what I described before it reaches the cut.
Often, this treatment has replaced the need for a cut. I have tried it, which is to take a curved iron tool from steel that has the following shape:.
The tip of the instrument is a sharp pointed one introduced into the stick, then take a thread and tie it to the penis below the stone so that it will not return to the bladder, and introduce the blade gently into the urethra until the bladder reaches the same stone.
And you turn the bladder with your hand on the stone little by little as you aim to pierce it until it passes through from the other side, for then urine flows from its location and you press your hand on what remains of the stone from outside the penis, so that it crumbles and comes out with the urine and the ailment is cured.
If this treatment does not present itself to you because of an obstacle that hinders you from it, then tie a thread below the stone and another thread above the stone, and then cut through the stone in the same penis between the two threads and remove it.
Then you remove the thread and clean the dried blood that has become in the wound, but it is necessary to tie the thread below the stone so that it does not return to the bladder, and the other thread from above so that when the thread is removed after the removal of the stone, the skin returns to its place to cover the wound.
And therefore it is necessary for you, when you tie the upper thread, to raise the skin above so that it returns when you finish and covers the wound as we said.
Chapter Sixty-One.
On extracting stones from women.
Stones rarely develop in women, but if one of them has a stone, it is difficult to treat and is prevented for many reasons: one is that the woman may be a virgin, and the second is that you do not find a woman who permits herself to the physician.
If she is a virgin or one of the protected, and the third is that you do not find a woman who excels in this craft, especially the work with the hands, and the fourth is that the location of the cut on the stone from women is far from the location of the stone, so it needs a deep incision.
In that danger, if necessity demands it, there is a need for an expert female physician, and rarely are they found. If you cannot find one, then seek a chaste, trustworthy male physician or get a skilled midwife who is knowledgeable in the affairs of women, or a woman who has some indication of proficiency in this profession.
Prepare her and order her to do all that you command her of examining for stones, first of all, seeing if the woman is a virgin; it is necessary that she insert her finger into her vagina and examine for stones, if she finds them press them under her finger.
Then, order her to make an incision on her, if she is not a virgin but has had intercourse, order the midwife to insert her finger into the vagina of the patient and examine for stones after placing her left hand on the bladder and squeezing it well.
If she finds them, it is necessary that she push them from the mouth of the bladder downwards as far as her strength allows until she ends with them at the root of the thigh, then make an incision on her opposite half of the vagina at the root of the thigh from whichever side she feels the stone.
And her finger does not move from the stone, pressed under it, let the incision be small first, then she inserts a probe into that small incision, if she feels the stone, she increases the incision to the extent she knows the stone will come out of it, and know that there are many kinds of stones.
Some are small and large, smooth and rough, long and rounded, and have a notch; so know their types so you can deduce what you want. If blood overwhelms you, throw powdered alum into the wound and hold it for an hour until the bleeding stops, then return to your work.
Until the stone comes out, and do that you count among the instruments mentioned in removing stones from men to help you in your work, if excessive bleeding overpowers you and you know by the pulse of blood that it is from a severed artery, place the cauterizer on the wound.
Fix it with the forceps firmly and leave it, do not interfere with it, leave the stone and do not remove it, for perhaps it will cause harm to the patient. Then treat the wound, and when the bleeding has subsided after days and the area is healed, return to your work until the stone is removed.
The second sixty chapter.
On an incision on the water-bearing vein.
The water-bearing vein is a gathering of moisture in the white peritoneum which is under the skin of the scrotum surrounding the testicle and is called the tunica vaginalis, and it may be in a special membrane prepared by nature on one side of the testicle.
Until he thinks that it is another testicle and it is between the skin of the scrotum and the white peritoneum which we have mentioned, and this does not happen except rarely, and this vein is generated from weakness exposed to women, so that they put this material in place, and it may be exposed due to a blow on the woman.
And this moisture is of many colors, either its color is yellowish, or it may be red like blood, or dark black like gall, or white like water and it is the most common, and the signs by which it is known.
Where the water meets, if it is in the white peritoneum which we have mentioned, the swelling is round to a slight length like the shape of an egg and the testicle does not appear because the moisture surrounds it from all sides.
And if the moisture is in a special membrane for it, the swelling is round on one side of the testicle.
And for this reason, a person imagines it to be another testicle, and if the moisture is between the skin of the scrotum and the white peritoneum, then it is located under the touch, but if you want to know the color of the moisture, aspirate the swelling with the square probe which we have shown its image, and whatever comes out in the wake of the probe, judge it by what is inside.
When we come to treat with iron, it is necessary to order the patient to bleed if he can do so, and seeing his body full, then he lies on his back on something slightly high, and you place under him a lot of shavings, then you sit on his left.
And order a servant to sit on his right, extending his penis to one side of the scrotum and toward the navel region, then take a wide scalpel and cut the scrotum from the middle lengthwise to near the genitals.
And make the incision straight, parallel to the line that divides the scrotum in half until it reaches the white peritoneum, then peel it and be careful not to cut through it, and your peeling of it from the side that adheres to the testicle should be more, and you explore the peeling as much as you can.
Then, empty the peritoneum filled with fluid with a wide spatula and extract all the water, then separate the edges of the incision with spatulas and extend the peritoneum upward without touching the scrotum containing it, and cut the peritoneum as much as you can, either in one piece or in pieces.
And especially its thin side, for if you do not thoroughly cut it, you will not ensure that the water does not return. If the testicle appears outside its skin during your work, then when you finish cutting the peritoneum, fold it back and gather the edges of the scrotum with sutures.
Then treat him as you would any other surgery until it heals, and if you find that the testicle has rotted from another disease, then it is necessary to tie the vessels in the spermatic cord to prevent bleeding, then cut off the testicle from the spermatic cord and extract the testicle, then treat it as mentioned above.
If the water collected in both sides, know that they are both infected, so cut the other side as you did with the first one, and if it suits you to do the work together, then do so, then wipe away the blood.
Into the incisions, you introduce a sponge that has been soaked in oil or rose butter and make it from outside a second sponge which has been soaked in wine and oil and spread it on the testicles and observe the abdomen and place above a folded linen cloth called the refarid. And tie it from above with the bandage which is six-sided as in this image.
Then take two linen cloths and sew them and stuff them with cotton wool as in this example, and make the ends which are tied with cotton or wet wool and gather by pulling it into a trouser belt, and one end takes on the buttock to the back.
And the second takes to the groin and the two ends on the thighs from below and the remaining two on the hipbones, and gather all the pulling in a trouser belt, and this band can also be made with silk instead of cutting with iron.
And it is that you take a small, fine scalpel and cut with it the scrotum skin while it is protected as we described until the white peritoneum containing water is revealed then take another scalpel like this.
And it is like the Greek eye, then you apply it to that peritoneum and it is protected until all moisture comes out, then extend the peritoneum with the sutures and scrape with the scalpel the layer containing it and cut it according to what is possible for you until all of it is uprooted and protect from the egg do not touch it with fire.
And know that this work is safer and further from bleeding than the work with the cut, if something obstructs you in the vein of the cut or while using silk, a hot tumor or bleeding or anything else, then it is necessary to treat whatever hinders you with the treatment that suits it as previously mentioned.
If the patient is cowardly and does not endure this work because of his fear, then let him use the poultice as I describe it, and if it agrees with you according to what we have presented from the evidence.
The abscess is watery, so it is necessary to make the patient sit on a raised chair and then drain the swelling at its base with a wide scalpel. Make the incision along the body and make it wide enough for all the water to drain out. Then place a bandage on the site and tie it.
Leave it to drain the rest of the water, then treat it until the wound heals. If the water discharge stops while you are draining it, this is because the white membrane obstructs the mouth of the wound and prevents the water from coming out.
Then, it is necessary to insert a feather or the instrument used to drain water from love affairs, whose image has been presented earlier, or widen the incision slightly.
Be aware that the water may return and collect after about six months. If it collects, drain it in the same manner and have the patient rest during this time.
Chapter Thirty-Sixth.
On the incision for a fleshy abscess and its treatment.
Know that an incision on this type of abscess is a dangerous path leading to death in most cases, so we see it left alone and protected from it. I am describing its work and types of swelling.
I say that many swellings can occur in the bodies of women, and this is due to many reasons, either from excess heat that settles in the female areas, or from a blow. The color of the swelling is like the color of the body and there is no water in it.
It may be hardened, and perhaps the swelling is a hard lump that has the color of lead and feels nothing. It may also be from the entanglement of veins and their swelling as previously mentioned, or from the swelling of the veins. If it is caused by the swelling of the arteries, this is known as the dispersal of the swelling.
If you press it with your fingers, and it should not be exposed to the scalpel, as for that which is caused by the swelling of the veins, nothing spreads from it when pressed with the fingers. This type may be able to be incised and on all flesh.
This consists of cutting the skin of the scrotum and then stretching the testicle upward and bringing it out from the white membrane and freeing the spermatic cord from the vessels, tying the vessels and cutting the spermatic cord after having freed it from every side of the testicle, if the testicle has adhered to that nascent flesh.
Where the testicle should be brought out and cut, and if there is adhesion between something from the membranes or among the vessels, it is necessary to free all that adhesion and cut it with a circular incision.
If the flesh growth is in the place of adhesion that occurs from behind, it is necessary to cut all of it and bring out the testicle as we have said. When you have completed your work, wash the wound with wool soaked in rose butter and syrup, then treat it with all other treatment until it heals.
Chapter forty-sixth.
In the treatment of the boil that is with a varicose vein.
A varicose vein is a swelling twisted like a bunch of grapes with loosening of the veins, and it makes it difficult for the patient to move, exercise, and walk. In the treatment of this ailment, most of what was mentioned before is close to what is practiced.
But it is necessary to mention what the ancients did in treating it. I say that it is necessary for the patient to sit on a raised chair, then push the spermatic cord downward, and hold the scrotum with your fingers along with the vessels that are near the penis.
And let a servant hold it and stretch it strongly, then cut with a wide, sharp scalpel a curved incision along the vessels until the vessels are exposed, then peel them from every side as I have mentioned to you in the case of the arteries that are in the groin, and then insert a needle with a twisted thread into them.
Bind it at the first places where it was shown to you, and bind it also at its end, then cut it open in the middle with a vertical incision along the length of the body, and take out what has gathered in it of the cloudy corrupted fluids.
Then treat the abscess with the treatment of all other wounds that you want to develop in order for the vessels feeding one of the eggs to fall off, there is no harm in this, if the follicle presents itself to all the vessels, then it is necessary to remove one of the eggs along with the vessels so that it does not deprive the egg of nourishment. Before cutting off the vessels it wilts and there is no benefit from it.
Chapter fifty-sixth.
In the Treatment of  the Abdominal Abscess.
The occurrence of this abscess is from a tear that appears in the peritoneum extended on the abdomen near the flanks of the abdomen, so the intestine protrudes from that hernia into one of the eggs.
And this hernia is either from a tear in the peritoneum or from its extension, and these two types occur due to many reasons, either a blow or a jump or a shout or lifting something heavy and so on, and its sign if it is from the extension of the peritoneum that it happens little by little over a long time.
And it does not happen suddenly, and the swelling is level to about the depth before the peritoneum compresses the intestine, and its sign if it is from a tear in the peritoneum that it happens from the beginning with great pain at once, and the swelling is different appearing under the skin nearby.
And that by the intestine coming out and its destination outside of the peritoneum, and it may come out with the appendix, and this abscess is called abdominal and appendicular, and it may be with gas, and there may be pus in the intestine and it gets trapped there, so it leads to the death of the patient.
For it causes a hard pain and a cracking, especially if pressed, and the treatment of these types of ailment with iron is dangerous so you should be wary of falling into it. The method is to order the sick person to return the intestines with his hand inside his belly if they come back.
Then he lies on his side between your hands and raises his legs, then you extend the skin that is below the rib to above and split the entire foreskin lengthwise, then you insert pliers into the edges of the incision as much as needed to open it with them.
And the incision should be as much as an egg can come out of, then you peel off the membranes under the foreskin until if the white, hard peritoneum is revealed on every side, then insert your index finger into what is below the egg.
Between the white peritoneum under the egg and the second peritoneum, and with this you release the adhesions that are behind the egg, then bend it with the right hand into inside the foreskin, and with this extend the white peritoneum upwards with the left hand and raise the egg with the peritoneum towards the incision.
And order the servant to extend the egg upwards and you release the adhesions behind it completely and search with your finger so that there is nothing from the twisted intestines in the white, hard peritoneum, if you find something from it, push it into the belly below.
Then take a needle with a thick thread that has been twisted from ten threads and insert it at the end of the peritoneum under the foreskin that is next to the incision, then cut the ends of the folded thread until there are four threads. Then weave some of them together in a crisscross pattern and tie the peritoneum that we said is under the foreskin with a strong knot on both sides, then also wrap the ends of the threads and tie them with a tight knot so that nothing from the vessels that nourish it can reach it. So that a hot tumor may not appear, and there also may be made a second ligature outside the first ligature, farther from it by less than two fingers' breadth. And after these two ligatures, draw from the peritoneum under the skin of the scrotum as much as the thickness of a finger.
So that a hot tumor may not appear, and there also may be made a second ligature outside the first ligature, farther from it by less than two fingers' breadth. And after these two ligatures, draw from the peritoneum under the skin of the scrotum as much as the thickness of a finger. And cut the rest of it all in a circular fashion and remove with it the testicle, then split beneath the skin of the scrotum a split which will drain blood and fluid as we described previously. Then, cotton dipped in oil is applied to the wound, and the ligature we described is used.
And the white peritoneum which we mentioned after cutting it may be cauterized, carefully avoiding bleeding, as this often occurs. The ligature is left until it falls off of its own accord; if its falling off is delayed, let hot water be applied to it and what causes perspiration be placed on it until it falls off.
Then the wound is treated with all the treatments for wounds until it heals.
Chapter Sixty-Sixth.
In the case of this hernia, I have not seen anyone dare to treat it with iron. The earlier authors stated that it should be treated like the hernia with a testicle, namely by gently tying off the vessels after making an incision beneath them.
Then, it is split in the middle, and the tumor is treated with what opens it until the vessels fall out, and the wound is treated as we have mentioned until it heals.
Chapter Seventy-Sixth.
In the hernia that occurs in the groin.
A hernia may occur in the groin as we mentioned, where the contents are not protruded and nothing descends from the intestines into it; if it does descend, it is easily returned at all times.
But if it persists for a long time, the opening in the peritoneum becomes larger until the intestines and omentum descend into the scrotum, which occurs due to the extension of the peritoneum that is present in the groin, as we mentioned previously. This is because the peritoneum extends and then relaxes and the place sags, and its treatment by cauterization as I have previously described.
And it can be treated with iron in this manner, which is that the patient lies on his back between your hands, and then you cut the place of the hernia that appears as a longitudinal incision according to three fingersâ€™ width, and then you cover the peritoneum under the skin.
Until the white peritoneum underneath is exposed, then you take a thread and place it on the place that has come from the peritoneum and press it into the depth of the abdomen, and then sew the two places that have resulted at the end of the thread from the peritoneum and glue them together with stitches.
Then you pull on the end of the thread and do not cut the peritoneum at all, nor touch the egg or anything else as I have taught you in the treatment of inguinal hernias, then treat it with the treatment of surgical wounds.
If the threads are cut off, clean them and close the wound until it heals, for the peritoneum contracts and does not increase the protrusion of the hernia.
And cauterization is best in this place because it is closer to safety.
Chapter Eighty-Sixth.
In the relaxation of the scrotum skin.
The skin of the scrotum often relaxes in some people without relaxing the flesh inside it, and its appearance is ugly, so whoever desires to treat it should put the patient to sleep on his back.
And cut all the skin that has relaxed on the thick skin, and then bring together the edges, and if you wish to sew first the excess of the relaxed skin with three or four stitches and make sure of the stitch, then cut between the stitches.
Then treat it with the treatment of all surgical wounds until it heals and the stitches are removed.
Chapter Ninety-Six
On castration.
Castration is forbidden in our Law.
For this reason, it behooved me not to mention it in this book of mine, but I have mentioned it for two reasons: one is that this should be in the knowledge of the physician if he is asked about it and that he may know the treatment of him who has undergone it. And the other reason is that we often need to castrate some animals for our benefit.
As with sheep, goats, and cats, and the like of animals. I say that castration is done in two ways: either by softening or by cutting. As for the one done by softening, its method is that we immerse the animal in hot water until its testes relax and soften and hang down.
Then you soften it with your hand until it dissolves and is not palpable to the touch. As for castration by cutting, it behooves you to grasp the animal and squeeze the scrotum with your left hand, then tie the spermatic cords and make a single incision on each testicle.
Until the two testicles appear, then cut them after you have removed their coverings and leave nothing on them except for the thin sac that is on the vessels. This type of castration is better than the one done by softening.
Because softening may leave something of the female organs, and the animal may then desire copulation. Then you treat the wound until it heals.
Chapter Seventy
On treating hermaphrodites.
A hermaphrodite in men comes in two types: one is that a shape appears similar to a female genitalia, with hair, below the scrotum or in the skin between the male organs, and urine may flow from what is in the scrotal skin.
As for women, there is one type and it appears above the vulva on the pubic bone, like small male penises protruding outward, one resembling a man's penis and the two resembling female genitalia.
The two types of men and the one type of woman it is necessary to cut away the excess flesh until its trace disappears, then treat them with the treatment of all other wounds until they heal. As for the second type of man from whom urine comes out that is in the skin of the scrotum there is no work done on him, nor does he recover at all.
Chapter seventy-one.
On cutting the clitoris and the flesh that comes from the vagina of women.
The clitoris may increase in size beyond the natural amount until it becomes noticeable and spoils its appearance, and it may become enlarged in some women to the extent that it spreads like men's and becomes involved in intercourse.
It is necessary to grasp the tip of the clitoris with your hand or a clamp and cut it, but do not be excessive in cutting, especially at the depth of its root so that it does not cause bleeding.
Then treat it with the treatment of wounds until it heals, and as for the growing flesh, it is flesh that grows in the mouth of the womb until it fills it.
And perhaps it comes out to the outside, like a navel. And therefore some of the ancients call it the umbilical disease, so it is necessary to cut it like the clitoris, and treat it until it heals.
Chapter seventy-two.
On treating hernias.
Hernia is when the vagina of a woman is not pierced or the opening is small, and it may be natural from birth or acquired. The acquired one comes from a cause that has progressed, and it may be from excess growing flesh.
Or from a thin or thick peritoneum, and it may be in the depth of the womb or its sides or above or below it, and it prevents intercourse, the cord, and childbirth, and perhaps menstruation. And knowing this is by looking at it with the midwife.
If the obstruction is visible and close, then if it is not visible, search for it with your fingers or a probe. If the obstruction is from thin peritoneum and is close to the sword-like parts, quickly rupture it by making on the sword-like parts a shape like the ribs then place your thumbs of both hands on it.
And the woman on her back, spreading her legs, then extend the sword-like parts with force until the thin peritoneum is ruptured and the obstruction opens, then take a piece of cloth and soak it in oil and put it on the place, and mate with the woman every day so that the place does not close again.
If the peritoneum is thick and dense, it should be incised with a wide scalpel resembling a leaf of reed. If the obstruction is from growing flesh, tie it with forceps and cut it off. And let there be with you medicine that stops bleeding without pain like myrrh, frankincense, and mastic mixed with egg white.
Then use a wide lead pipe so that the wound does not close quickly, hold it for days and use a piece of dry linen, then treat it with all the treatment of hematoma until it heals. It may occur in the uterus another growth of flesh, then it should be cut off in this way.
Unless it is a cancerous tumor, for the cancerous tumor that is in the uterus should not be touched with iron at all.
Chapter Seventy-Three.
In the treatment of hemorrhoids, warts, and red pimples that appear in women's genitals.
As for hemorrhoids, it is a swelling of the mouths of the veins until much blood flows from them constantly. If hemorrhoids are advanced, they become warts. And I have mentioned in the classification their types, signs, and we mention here.
What accepts treatment from them and what does not accept treatment, I say that hemorrhoids and warts if they are in the depth of the uterus and do not appear to the touch there is no treatment with iron. And what is from them at the mouth of the uterus that is felt it is the one that is treated.
It is necessary that the woman enters a cold house and then spreads out the warts with a file or a rough cloth and cuts them from their roots, then she applies [something] to them when blood flows from one of the cutting points for bleeding without any teasing.
Like frankincense, mastic, benzoin, and the like. Then she raises her legs to the wall for an hour then lets them down into cold water. If the bleeding persists, then have her sit in a decoction of  sumac, pomegranate peel, and hawthorn, etc., then take barley flour and knead it with honey and vinegar.
And spread it on her back and if the bleeding stops, otherwise, apply a poultice to the chest and armpits without condition, then take a piece of cloth and dip it in the juice of  mallow, or the juice of kidâ€™s tongue, or the juice of hawthorn sprigs with a syrup of hawthorn, and apply it to the area.
And if the tumor subsides, treat the area with an ointment until it heals. As for the red scab, it resembles the tops of the rough-looking  sparrow's heads, so it is necessary to cut what has appeared from it according to what I mentioned regarding warts and treat it until it heals.
Chapter Seventy-Four.
On the abscess that appears in the womb.
Many kinds of tumors may appear in the womb, such as cancer,  hard tumor, ulcers, polyps, carbuncles,  fistulas, hemorrhoids, fissures, warts, and hot tumors. I have mentioned all of these diseases and their types and symptoms in the previous section.
It is necessary to mention in this article the hot tumor that appears in the womb if it is one of the tumors that gather over time, how its treatment with iron is done. You should examine it and see if the pain of the tumor at its beginning is sharp with throbbing, inflammation, and fever.
And if you see it red when touched, do not hurry to treat it and treat it with what helps ripening until when these symptoms subside, then it is necessary that the woman sit on a chair with two seats and leans against her back.
And she gathers her legs to the side of the lower abdomen and her thighs are spread apart, and her arms become under her knees, and they are tied with a bandage that is suitable.
Therefore, then the midwife sits on the right side and uses the instrument that opens the mouth of the womb, whose image will come later, and it is necessary if you want to use this tool to estimate the depth of a woman's womb so that what enters from the instrument is not more than the depth of the womb.
And it will hurt the woman if the instrument is more than the depth, then it is necessary to put a rest on the edge of the cervix to prevent the whole instrument from entering into the depth of the womb, and the spiral that runs in the instrument should be from the upper side.
And you hold the instrument and the servant rotates the spiral until it opens the cervix, and if the opening appears and feels soft and tender, then it is necessary to cut it at its head with a wide scalpel, and when the entire time has been emptied.
Then it is necessary that a soft thread soaked in rose butter or green oil with some of the essence be inside the wound, and the thread should come out from the cut in the cervix, and cotton wool clean, soaked in water that has been boiled with baker's yeast, should be placed on the outside of the womb and on the vulva.
Then it is treated after two days with the ointment that is suitable for it until it heals.
And the womb and the wound may be washed by injecting water and honey, then with water that has been boiled with the root of saffron or long turmeric, then it returns to the ointment, if the opening was hidden inside the womb.
It is necessary that you refrain from treating it with iron but rather treat it with what has been mentioned in the division.
The Fifth and Seventy Chapter.
In teaching the caul, how to treat the live ones if they come out contrary to their natural form.
It is necessary for the midwife to know first the natural form of childbirth, for from its signs if you see the woman strain downwards and yearn to smell the air and ease what she is on from delivery.
And it hastens the exit of the fetus, know that this childbirth is in its natural form and his exit is on his head and the placenta with him or hanging from his navel, so if you see these signs, it is necessary to squeeze her belly so that the fetus may exit quickly.
For if it descends on its head, the placenta descends with him and is cleansed from that filth with a good cleansing, and what besides this childbirth is not natural, it is condemned because the fetus may come out on its legs and its hands come out before its head and its legs.
And one hand or one leg or he comes out with his head and hand or comes out curled up, and perhaps turns on his back and similar to those condemned forms, so it is necessary for the midwife to be skillful and gentle with all these things and beware of error and mistake.
And I make clear each form of it and how the trick is in it so that you may infer from it and stand on it, if the fetus comes out on its head, the natural exit, and it intensified on the woman, and it was difficult for her to give birth, and you see her strength has weakened, so sit her on a stool and order women to hold her firm.
And comfort her womb with boiled cumin and wet date poultice, then the midwife enters between her fingers a small scalpel and tears open the placenta with it or tears it with her fingernail until what is in it of moisture flows out, and she squeezes the woman's belly until the fetus descends.
If it does not descend, it is necessary to inject the woman with licorice saliva mixed with butter of shierj. Then order her after the injection to strain and sneeze with a kandis. Hold her mouth and nose, for the fetus will come out within an hour. If the hand of the fetus comes out first, it is necessary to return it gently little by little.
If it does not come to enter, place the woman on a platform and raise her legs above. Then shake the platform on the ground and the woman grasps so that she does not fall during the shaking. If the hands do not enter and the fetus dies, cut them and pull out the rest of the fetus.
Or tie his hands with a cloth and pull them moderately, for it will come out. The exit of the fetus on its legs, if the fetus comes out on its legs, then it is necessary to push its legs upwards and then turn the fetus little by little until it is straightened. Then take one of its legs and stretch it gradually.
If they came out to the thighs, order her to strain and sneeze with a kandis for it will come out. If it does not come out as described above, then return the fetus little by little until you make it in its natural shape, then it will come out smoothly at that time. If it is prevented from all that has been described.
Take saliva of khitmi, licorice saliva, butter of shierj and a boiled solution and strike them all in the mortar with good striking. Then apply it to the woman's genitals and lower belly. Then seat her in lukewarm water until the cervix reaches.
If you see that it has loosened below her, then make for her a pillow from marr and she carries it. If she holds the pillow for an hour, then seat her on the chair, then sneeze her and block her mouth and nose and squeeze her lower belly with gentle squeezing. For the fetus will come out within an hour. The exit of the fetus on its knees and hands.
If it emerges in this manner, insert your hands gradually into the vagina and then place the woman on her side. Let her legs hang down as she lies on a bed, fold your arms and gently press above her abdomen little by little. Then withdraw what is beneath her legs from the cushions until she is positioned downwards. If the fetus does not emerge, take both her legs and move them vigorously. Then press above the pubic bone little by little until the fetus ascends upwards. Then the midwife inserts her hand and smooths the fetus gradually.
Tell the woman to strain until the fetus emerges. If the fetus emerges with one hand extended, put your hand back in and withdraw it. If you cannot withdraw it, place the woman upright and make her walk. If she cannot walk, have her lie down.
Place her on a bed and shake her legs vigorously. Then use the forceps described from the instruments. If she takes hold of it, seat her on a chair and treat to withdraw the hand and smooth the fetus in its natural form.  Help the woman cough and tell her to strain until it emerges.
The fetus emerges on its side, with outstretched hands and its face toward its motherâ€™s back. The midwife must grasp the childâ€™s hand and turn it gradually, smoothing it gently. If it is straightened, apply the fat and instruments described above to its chest.
Then tell her to move slightly. If she does so, seat her on a chair and tell her to lean to the right side. Then tell her to strain and cough with the forceps because it will emerge.
If it descends into the vagina with the placenta, cut the placenta open with your fingernail until it is freed of moisture. If it adheres to the childâ€™s face or neck, cut it from the umbilical cord so that it does not choke and die. Then push the child inside until it assumes its proper position.
Tell the woman to give birth several times, for it is an easy exit, the exit of twins or many fetuses. Know that twins are often born and may be born three or four. They live unless this is rare. As for five, it is something outside nature, they do not live at all.
And they are surrounded by a single placenta, even if many, and they are separated by a thin partition between them, attached to the cord of each one of them.  And they may exit as one fetus exits in an easy natural way, and they may exit with difficulty as we described.
If the birth of some of them is difficult and becomes what we mentioned from unnatural shapes, treat it as we described. And let the midwife be gentle and do what she does with softness and patience and find a way for every shape according to what is suitable for her that leads to safety,.
Mention what is imagined in the womb of fetuses that fall, they may be imagined in the womb one and two and three and four and five and six and seven and more than ten, it has been proven to me that a woman miscarried seven and another fifteen, all of them imagined like this.
By the estimation of the Exalted, All-Knowing, all of this should be in the knowledge of the midwife because perhaps something like this may happen to her one day so she can meet it with what is appropriate.
Chapter Sixty-Seven.
On the extraction of a dead fetus.
If you treated the dead fetus with what was mentioned in the division of treatment and it did not come out, and compelled you to work with your hand, then it is necessary for you to look. If the woman is healthy in strength and there is nothing from the symptoms that one fears harming her, then it is necessary for the woman to lie down on a bed on her back.
And her head is tilted down and her legs are raised, and a servant adjusts her from both sides or ties her to the bed so that her body does not be drawn when the fetus is pulled.
Then she moistens the mouth of the womb with moist pastes along with saliva of catmint and fenugreek and linseed, then the midwife anoints her hand with these pastes and saliva and gently inserts it into the womb, then she seeks a place in which to insert the forceps from the fetus, and the places that correspond to it.
Look if the fetus is positioned so that it descends headfirst, she inserts the forceps in its eyes or cheekbones or mouth or chin or under its beard or throat or in the places near the ribs or under the scapulae.
But if it descends on its legs, then in the groin and middle ribs, she should hold the forceps in her right hand and make its curve between the fingers of her left hand and gently insert her hand and insert a forceps in some of those places mentioned.
Until she reaches something empty, then she inserts another or third forceps if needed so that the pull is equal and does not tilt in one direction, then she pulls with a steady pull and it is not just on a straight line but moves to every direction.
To make it easier to exit as it is done with the molar when pulling it out, and it is necessary between that to relax the pull. If it gets stuck in one direction, then the midwife should anoint some of her fingers with oil and insert them from that side to turn what is stuck.  If some of the fetus exits, then the forceps are moved to other places.
She raises it slightly and does this until the whole fetus exits, if a hand comes out before the others and it cannot be put back because of its tightness then it is necessary to wrap it in a cloth and pull it until all of it exits, then cut it.
If it is in the wrist joint or in the elbow and thus you should do in the other hand and in both legs, if the head of the child is large and there was pressure on its exit or there was water gathered in its head, then it is necessary to insert between the fingers a pointed scalpel.
And you split it with it the head and the water comes out or you smoke it with the tool that is called the  misdaq which its image comes with the images of all the tools in the chapter after this one.
Likewise you do if the child is large headed by nature, then it is necessary to split the skull or smooth it with the misdaq as we said, then you extract the bones with pliers. If the head came out and contracted at the collarbone, let him split until the moisture in the chest is poured out.
For then the chest joins, and if the chest did not join and it was not possible to exit, cut a piece as much as you can. If the lower abdomen is warm or there is a boil in it, then it is necessary to pound it until the moisture flows out of it.
If the child is on its legs, then pulling it is easy and straightening it into the mouth of the womb is easy. If it contracted at the abdomen or chest, then it is necessary to pull it with a rope that you wrapped around your hand and split the abdomen or chest until what is in them flows out.
If you extracted all the organs and the head remained and was held back, let the midwife enter her left hand, if the mouth of the womb is open, then she enters her hand into the neck of the womb and seeks with it the head and pulls it with her fingers into the mouth of the womb, then she enters a rope or two ropes into it and pulls it with them.
If the mouth of the womb has closed due to a hot tumor, it should not be forced upon, but rather at that time it is necessary to use the pouring of wet, fatty things and it is used to sit in water that softens and moistens.
As for if the fetus is on its side, and if it is possible to straighten it, then use what was mentioned regarding a live fetus. If that is not possible, then cut it in sections and remove it, and it is necessary that nothing of the placenta be left inside at all. When you have finished treating it, then use what was mentioned from treatment for hot tumors that appear in the wombs.
If bleeding occurs, then lower it in holding waters and use the rest of the treatment. I have seen a woman who had become pregnant, the fetus died within her, then she became pregnant with it again.
Then the other fetus died as well. After a long time, a tumor appeared in her womb and it swelled until it opened and discharged pus. I was called to treat her, and I treated her for a long time but the wound did not close. So I placed some strong drawing ointments on it.
Then bone came out of the place, and after some days another bone came out. I was amazed by this because the abdomen is a place with no bones. I estimated that it was from the bones of the dead fetus, so I searched the wound and extracted many bones from the head of the fetus.
And I continued to do so until I extracted many bones from her. The woman is in the best of health, and she lived like this for a while, pus would continue to come out from the place, but I bring you this rare case here.
Because there is knowledge and assistance in what the physician who creates with his hand attempts to do for treatment.
Chapter Seventy-Seven.

Their width is about a finger, and their length is a palm and a half. And in the middle of the two pieces there are grooves, from the same kind of wood as the pieces themselves, bound into them. Their length is half a palm or a little more, and their width is about two fingers or a little more. These are the grooves.
They are the ones that enter the mouth of the womb to open it when you maneuver the forceps. A picture of another tool similar to this, more delicate and lighter:
